69|f160e2|    let content: Content
70|b4687f|    
71|ca8c99|    init(@ViewBuilder content: () -> Content) {
72|0bc2b5|        self.content = content()
73|27e597|    }
74|b4687f|    
75|5ed0a9|    func makeUIViewController(context: Context) -> KeyCommandController {
76|6b6e02|        let controller = KeyCommandController()
77|5a4a2c|        let host = UIHostingController(rootView: content)

8|adc83b|

10|404b8d|- `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` (removed inline structs)
11|eceecc|- `Commands/AppCommands.swift` (not used in .commands{})
12|0fca8d|- `Views/Editor/SyntaxHighlightingTextView.swift` (only editor-specific shortcuts like Tab, Escape)

127|adc83b|
128|586e24|If you see "keyboard shortcut already in use" warnings:
129|adc83b|
130|244022|1. Check that `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` does NOT define inline menu structs
131|1275d8|2. Check that the Menus/ folder files are the ONLY place defining these Commands structs
132|134003|3. Ensure `AppCommands.swift` is NOT included in `.commands {}` block

1400|2baf81|            guard let self = self else { return }

2|adc83b|
3|d3c0c9|**IMPORTANT: This document defines where ALL keyboard shortcuts are implemented.**
4|adc83b|
5|a26f0d|## Architecture
6|adc83b|
7|f1502e|Keyboard shortcuts are defined in ONE place only: the `Menus/` folder.
8|adc83b|
9|151a17|**DO NOT** define duplicate shortcuts in:
10|404b8d|- `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` (removed inline structs)
11|eceecc|- `Commands/AppCommands.swift` (not used in .commands{})
12|0fca8d|- `Views/Editor/SyntaxHighlightingTextView.swift` (only editor-specific shortcuts like Tab, Escape)
13|841346|- `Views/Editor/MultiCursorTextView.swift` (inherits from SyntaxHighlightingTextView)
14|adc83b|

5|a26f0d|## Architecture
6|adc83b|
7|f1502e|Keyboard shortcuts are defined in ONE place only: the `Menus/` folder.

[read_file]
snapshot: 96703e061c21
File: VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS_SOURCE_OF_TRUTH.md (lines 2-140 of 140)
────────────────────────────────────────
2|adc83b|
3|d3c0c9|**IMPORTANT: This document defines where ALL keyboard shortcuts are implemented.**
4|adc83b|
5|a26f0d|## Architecture
6|adc83b|
7|f1502e|Keyboard shortcuts are defined in ONE place only: the `Menus/` folder.
8|adc83b|
9|151a17|**DO NOT** define duplicate shortcuts in:
10|404b8d|- `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` (removed inline structs)
11|eceecc|- `Commands/AppCommands.swift` (not used in .commands{})
12|0fca8d|- `Views/Editor/SyntaxHighlightingTextView.swift` (only editor-specific shortcuts like Tab, Escape)
13|841346|- `Views/Editor/MultiCursorTextView.swift` (inherits from SyntaxHighlightingTextView)
14|adc83b|

126|f905d2|## Troubleshooting Duplicate Warnings
127|adc83b|
128|586e24|If you see "keyboard shortcut already in use" warnings:
129|adc83b|
130|244022|1. Check that `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` does NOT define inline menu structs
131|1275d8|2. Check that the Menus/ folder files are the ONLY place defining these Commands structs
132|134003|3. Ensure `AppCommands.swift` is NOT included in `.commands {}` block
133|adc83b|

135|3b731b|- ⌘ = Command
136|ea13de|- ⇧ = Shift  
137|699314|- ⌥ = Option/Alt
138|2c990c|- ⌃ = Control
139|2e2669|- ↑↓←→ = Arrow keys

1|60ac82|# Keyboard Shortcuts - Single Source of Truth
2|adc83b|
3|d3c0c9|**IMPORTANT: This document defines where ALL keyboard shortcuts are implemented.**
4|adc83b|
5|a26f0d|## Architecture
6|adc83b|
7|f1502e|Keyboard shortcuts are defined in ONE place only: the `Menus/` folder.
8|adc83b|
9|151a17|**DO NOT** define duplicate shortcuts in:
10|404b8d|- `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` (removed inline structs)
11|eceecc|- `Commands/AppCommands.swift` (not used in .commands{})
12|0fca8d|- `Views/Editor/SyntaxHighlightingTextView.swift` (only editor-specific shortcuts like Tab, Escape)
13|841346|- `Views/Editor/MultiCursorTextView.swift` (inherits from SyntaxHighlightingTextView)
14|adc83b|
15|adfa3f|## Source Files (Menus/ folder)
16|adc83b|

113|a1cba4|## Editor-Only Shortcuts (SyntaxHighlightingTextView.swift)
114|adc83b|
115|034c10|These are NOT menu shortcuts - they are UIKeyCommand for the text view only:
116|adc83b|
117|6ac725|| Shortcut | Action |
118|d2eab8||----------|--------|
119|7d1b9b|| ⌥D | Peek Definition |
120|7eca65|| Tab | Accept Autocomplete / Insert Tab |
121|78979e|| Escape | Dismiss Autocomplete/Peek |
122|62253d|| ⌘⌥[ | Fold Code |
123|88c910|| ⌘⌥] | Unfold Code |
124|b02f15|| ⌘⇧A | AI Assistant |
125|adc83b|
126|f905d2|## Troubleshooting Duplicate Warnings
127|adc83b|
128|586e24|If you see "keyboard shortcut already in use" warnings:
129|adc83b|
130|244022|1. Check that `VSCodeiPadOSApp.swift` does NOT define inline menu structs
131|1275d8|2. Check that the Menus/ folder files are the ONLY place defining these Commands structs
132|134003|3. Ensure `AppCommands.swift` is NOT included in `.commands {}` block
133|adc83b|
134|714ce8|## Symbol Legend
135|3b731b|- ⌘ = Command
136|ea13de|- ⇧ = Shift  
137|699314|- ⌥ = Option/Alt
138|2c990c|- ⌃ = Control
139|2e2669|- ↑↓←→ = Arrow keys

68|f2cec5|struct KeyCommandBridge<Content: View>: UIViewControllerRepresentable {
69|f160e2|    let content: Content
70|b4687f|    
71|ca8c99|    init(@ViewBuilder content: () -> Content) {
72|0bc2b5|        self.content = content()
73|27e597|    }
74|b4687f|    
75|5ed0a9|    func makeUIViewController(context: Context) -> KeyCommandController {
76|6b6e02|        let controller = KeyCommandController()
77|5a4a2c|        let host = UIHostingController(rootView: content)
78|0596a7|        host.view.backgroundColor = .clear
79|a81475|        controller.addChild(host)
80|285c40|        controller.view.addSubview(host.view)
81|e88a8e|        host.view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
82|c31f08|        NSLayoutConstraint.activate([
83|4f3c57|            host.view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.topAnchor),
84|0bc6fc|            host.view.bottomAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.bottomAnchor),
85|fff93c|            host.view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.leadingAnchor),
86|c81d03|            host.view.trailingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.trailingAnchor),
87|082e2d|        ])
88|604700|        host.didMove(toParent: controller)
89|1375d7|        return controller
90|27e597|    }
91|b4687f|    
92|04a02a|    func updateUIViewController(_ vc: KeyCommandController, context: Context) {
93|e1d69c|        if let host = vc.children.first as? UIHostingController<Content> {
94|dc185c|            host.rootView = content
95|5f3077|        }
96|27e597|    }

68|f2cec5|struct KeyCommandBridge<Content: View>: UIViewControllerRepresentable {
69|f160e2|    let content: Content
70|b4687f|    
71|ca8c99|    init(@ViewBuilder content: () -> Content) {
72|0bc2b5|        self.content = content()
73|27e597|    }
74|b4687f|    
75|5ed0a9|    func makeUIViewController(context: Context) -> KeyCommandController {
76|6b6e02|        let controller = KeyCommandController()
77|5a4a2c|        let host = UIHostingController(rootView: content)
78|0596a7|        host.view.backgroundColor = .clear
79|a81475|        controller.addChild(host)
80|285c40|        controller.view.addSubview(host.view)
81|e88a8e|        host.view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
82|c31f08|        NSLayoutConstraint.activate([
83|4f3c57|            host.view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.topAnchor),
84|0bc6fc|            host.view.bottomAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.bottomAnchor),
85|fff93c|            host.view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.leadingAnchor),
86|c81d03|            host.view.trailingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: controller.view.trailingAnchor),
87|082e2d|        ])
88|604700|        host.didMove(toParent: controller)
89|1375d7|        return controller
90|27e597|    }
91|b4687f|    
92|04a02a|    func updateUIViewController(_ vc: KeyCommandController, context: Context) {
93|e1d69c|        if let host = vc.children.first as? UIHostingController<Content> {
94|dc185c|            host.rootView = content
95|5f3077|        }
96|27e597|    }

89|8c7288|    var windowId: UUID {
90|efbf1b|        // Use persistentIdentifier to create a stable UUID

92|956e7f|            return uuid

100|968aa1|private extension Int {
101|04f38a|    var uuid: uuid_t {
102|db4b1b|        var value = self
103|7baffe|        var bytes = [UInt8](repeating: 0, count: 16)
104|8da4f9|        withUnsafeBytes(of: &value) { buffer in
105|615038|            for (index, byte) in buffer.enumerated() where index < 16 {
106|dadee0|                bytes[index] = byte
107|a7dc16|            }
108|5f3077|        }
109|80ab50|        return (bytes[0], bytes[1], bytes[2], bytes[3],
110|f2e7c9|                bytes[4], bytes[5], bytes[6], bytes[7],

500|ea8a39|extension UIResponder {
501|b4687f|    
502|06ecd9|    /// Registers keyboard commands for inline suggestions partial accept.
503|6a3cce|    /// Call this from your editor view controller to enable Ctrl+Right and Option+Right shortcuts.
504|05bcd9|    static func registerInlineSuggestionKeyCommands() -> [UIKeyCommand] {
505|d0ba57|        // Ctrl+Right Arrow for partial accept
506|4e4369|        let ctrlRightCommand = UIKeyCommand(
507|810d7f|            input: UIKeyCommand.inputRightArrow,
508|d08628|            modifierFlags: .control,
509|0e3f78|            action: #selector(performPartialAccept(_:))
510|3143a4|        )
511|b4eef5|        ctrlRightCommand.wantsPriorityOverSystemBehavior = true
512|d6ed84|        
513|6c4e41|        // Option+Right Arrow for partial accept (alternative binding)
514|c44b96|        let optRightCommand = UIKeyCommand(
515|810d7f|            input: UIKeyCommand.inputRightArrow,
516|722957|            modifierFlags: .alternate,
517|0e3f78|            action: #selector(performPartialAccept(_:))
518|3143a4|        )
519|67b4a4|        optRightCommand.wantsPriorityOverSystemBehavior = true
520|d6ed84|        
521|44f52a|        return [ctrlRightCommand, optRightCommand]
522|27e597|    }
523|b4687f|

525|a96529|        // Access the shared manager and perform partial accept
526|5e69c5|        // This requires the editor to insert the accepted text at cursor position
527|63edcc|        NotificationCenter.default.post(
528|ca72b7|            name: .inlineSuggestionPartialAccept,
529|b4da80|            object: nil
530|3143a4|        )
531|27e597|    }

109|b4687f|    
110|89e886|    // MARK: - Debounce & Search Task
111|ea971e|    @State private var searchTask: Task<Void, Never>?
112|370fcf|    @State private var debounceCancellable: AnyCancellable?
113|269f7f|    private let debounceInterval: DispatchQueue.SchedulerTimeType.Stride = .milliseconds(400)
114|b4687f|

123|276c10|    // MARK: - Sort & Filter State

125|3ee770|    @State private var sortAscending: Bool = true
126|d6760e|    @State private var selectedExtensions: Set<String> = []
127|bb7bcd|    @State private var groupByDirectory: Bool = false

135|b4687f|    
136|50903b|    // Binary file extensions to exclude
137|f1d796|    private let binaryExtensions = [".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png", ".gif", ".bmp", ".ico", ".pdf", ".zip", ".tar", ".gz", ".mp3", ".mp4", ".avi", ".mov", ".exe", ".dll", ".so", ".dylib", ".app", ".ipa", ".ipa", ".dmg", ".pkg", ".deb", ".rpm", ".img", ".iso", ".bin", ".dat", ".db", ".sqlite", ".sqlite3", ".ttf", ".otf", ".woff", ".woff2", ".eot"]

146|b4687f|    
147|f96259|    /// Returns the filtered, sorted, and limited results
148|f32b09|    var processedResults: [FileSearchResult] {
149|1a5bc0|        var filtered = rawResults
150|d6ed84|        
151|0a214d|        // 1. Filter by binary files
152|99c850|        if excludeBinaryFiles {
153|9b3c53|            filtered = filtered.filter { result in
154|74a475|                let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
155|979d9d|                return !binaryExtensions.contains(where: { $0.lowercased().hasSuffix(ext) })
156|a7dc16|            }
157|5f3077|        }
158|d6ed84|        
159|23706c|        // 2. Filter by selected extensions
160|8f0448|        if !selectedExtensions.isEmpty {
161|9b3c53|            filtered = filtered.filter { result in
162|74a475|                let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
163|db0fb9|                return selectedExtensions.contains { $0.lowercased().dropFirst() == ext }
164|a7dc16|            }
165|5f3077|        }
166|d6ed84|        
167|e35546|        // 3. Sort results
168|b5c3d5|        filtered = filtered.sorted { lhs, rhs in
169|cc07ab|            switch sortOption {
170|2eb58c|            case .fileName:
171|c61e48|                return sortAscending ? lhs.fileName < rhs.fileName : lhs.fileName > rhs.fileName
172|7a14db|            case .path:
173|8db7c1|                return sortAscending ? lhs.path < rhs.path : lhs.path > rhs.path
174|f24236|            case .matches:
175|beb3b2|                return sortAscending ? lhs.matches.count < rhs.matches.count : lhs.matches.count > rhs.matches.count
176|a7dc16|            }
177|5f3077|        }
178|d6ed84|        
179|b622d3|        // 4. Apply result limit
180|2f53d7|        if let maxCount = resultLimit.maxCount, filtered.count > maxCount {
181|78a06d|            filtered = Array(filtered.prefix(maxCount))
182|5f3077|        }
183|d6ed84|        
184|ed0d9a|        return filtered
185|27e597|    }
186|b4687f|    
187|afa680|    /// Group results by directory if enabled
188|bf562e|    var groupedResults: [(key: String, results: [FileSearchResult])] {
189|cfef88|        if groupByDirectory {
190|f958d9|            let grouped = Dictionary(grouping: processedResults) { $0.directory }
191|9c37af|            return grouped.sorted { $0.key < $1.key }.map { (key: $0.key, results: $0.value) }
192|b31999|        } else {
193|01a805|            return [(key: "", results: processedResults)]
194|5f3077|        }
195|27e597|    }
196|b4687f|    
197|7eee45|    /// All unique extensions from current results
198|8335d0|    var availableExtensions: [String] {
199|f40721|        let extensions = rawResults.map { (result: FileSearchResult) -> String in
200|b157b5|            let ext = (result.fileName as NSString).pathExtension
201|5a54b3|            return ext.isEmpty ? "noext" : ext.lowercased()
202|5f3077|        }
203|69f3ad|        return Array(Set(extensions)).sorted()
204|27e597|    }
205|b4687f|    
206|12bc82|    // MARK: - Keyboard Navigation Functions
207|b4687f|    
208|f6a132|    /// Builds the flat list of navigation items from results
209|e5849c|    private func buildNavigationItems() -> [SearchNavigationItem] {
210|ccfc3e|        var items: [SearchNavigationItem] = []
211|ad57e8|        let results = processedResults
212|ce48df|        for (fileIndex, fileResult) in results.enumerated() {
213|8e1a42|            for (matchIndex, match) in fileResult.matches.enumerated() {
214|e47853|                items.append(SearchNavigationItem(
215|ef8b8c|                    fileIndex: fileIndex,
216|e7bbe5|                    matchIndex: matchIndex,
217|ef4b99|                    fileID: fileResult.id,
218|a88193|                    matchID: match.id
219|2188d8|                ))
220|a7dc16|            }
221|5f3077|        }
222|1d239a|        return items
223|27e597|    }
224|b4687f|

255|b84c76|    /// Navigates to next result
256|639992|    private func navigateToNextResult() {
257|e554e3|        guard !navigationItems.isEmpty else { return }
258|d6ed84|        
259|82d91a|        if let current = selectedNavigationItem,
260|e6502a|           let currentIndex = navigationItems.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == current.id }) {
261|9ddba8|            let nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % navigationItems.count
262|59a7a6|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems[nextIndex]
263|b31999|        } else {
264|dec0e2|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems.first
265|5f3077|        }
266|27e597|    }
267|b4687f|    
268|56119f|    /// Navigates to previous result
269|8adb23|    private func navigateToPreviousResult() {
270|e554e3|        guard !navigationItems.isEmpty else { return }
271|d6ed84|        
272|82d91a|        if let current = selectedNavigationItem,
273|e6502a|           let currentIndex = navigationItems.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == current.id }) {
274|378834|            let prevIndex = (currentIndex - 1 + navigationItems.count) % navigationItems.count
275|c2bab4|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems[prevIndex]
276|b31999|        } else {
277|3109a0|            selectedNavigationItem = navigationItems.last
278|5f3077|        }
279|27e597|    }
280|b4687f|    
281|15b717|    /// Opens the currently selected result
282|a787fe|    private func openSelectedResult() {
283|f4616c|        guard let selected = selectedNavigationItem else { return }
284|ad57e8|        let results = processedResults
285|c8f72e|        guard selected.fileIndex < results.count else { return }
286|bdd740|        let fileResult = results[selected.fileIndex]
287|4f603d|        guard selected.matchIndex < fileResult.matches.count else { return }
288|08d2f8|        let match = fileResult.matches[selected.matchIndex]
289|e4b372|        onResultSelected?(fileResult.path, match.lineNumber)
290|27e597|    }

749|27e597|    }
750|b4687f|    
751|101550|    // MARK: - Debounced Search
752|b4687f|    
753|6320bf|    private func debouncedSearch(immediate: Bool = false) {
754|5ed5cb|        debounceCancellable?.cancel()
755|d6ed84|        
756|26b670|        if immediate {
757|47ed6c|            performDebouncedSearch(query: searchText)
758|b31999|        } else {
759|dcccb0|            setupDebouncedSearch()
760|5f3077|        }
761|27e597|    }
762|b4687f|    
763|1d3cf0|    private func performDebouncedSearch(query: String) {
764|798fdb|        searchTask?.cancel()
765|d6ed84|        
766|e78100|        guard query.count >= 2 else { return }
767|d6ed84|        
768|86191b|        let options = SearchManager.SearchOptions(
769|212967|            isCaseSensitive: matchCase,
770|d0fada|            isWholeWord: matchWholeWord,
771|31ed2c|            isRegex: useRegex
772|3143a4|        )
773|d6ed84|        
774|bed986|        let includeGlobs = filesToInclude
775|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
776|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
777|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
778|d6ed84|        
779|ce8d1a|        let excludeGlobs = filesToExclude
780|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
781|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
782|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
783|d6ed84|        
784|78ed4e|        let searchQuery = SearchManager.SearchQuery(
785|5f3d5e|            text: query,
786|62f7ee|            options: options,
787|ca52d5|            includeGlobs: includeGlobs,
788|f1536d|            excludeGlobs: excludeGlobs
789|3143a4|        )
790|d6ed84|        
791|6b2788|        searchTask = Task { [weak searchManager] in
792|597ee6|            guard let manager = searchManager else { return }
793|08ebed|            guard !Task.isCancelled else { return }
794|2e2a14|            manager.search(in: rootURL, query: searchQuery)
795|5f3077|        }
796|27e597|    }

812|eb174a|    private func performReplace() {
813|a606b5|        guard !searchText.isEmpty && !replaceText.isEmpty else { return }
814|d6ed84|        
815|86191b|        let options = SearchManager.SearchOptions(
816|212967|            isCaseSensitive: matchCase,
817|d0fada|            isWholeWord: matchWholeWord,
818|31ed2c|            isRegex: useRegex
819|3143a4|        )
820|d6ed84|        
821|bed986|        let includeGlobs = filesToInclude
822|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
823|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
824|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
825|d6ed84|        
826|ce8d1a|        let excludeGlobs = filesToExclude
827|646476|            .split(separator: ",")
828|6c985e|            .map { $0.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) }
829|c71ead|            .filter { !$0.isEmpty }
830|d6ed84|        
831|87daa1|        let query = SearchManager.SearchQuery(
832|29db41|            text: searchText,
833|62f7ee|            options: options,
834|ca52d5|            includeGlobs: includeGlobs,
835|f1536d|            excludeGlobs: excludeGlobs
836|3143a4|        )
837|d6ed84|        
838|0f1953|        Task {
839|71cc09|            do {
840|c52263|                let result = try await searchManager.replace(in: rootURL, query: query, replacement: replaceText)
841|71387f|                print("Replace completed: \(result.replacements) replacements in \(result.filesTouched) files")
842|91b9a2|            } catch {
843|e1dc9b|                print("Replace failed: \(error.localizedDescription)")
844|a7dc16|            }
845|5f3077|        }
846|27e597|    }
